fill-opacity="0.1"></path></g><defs><radialGradient id="radial-dark" cx="0" cy="0" r="1" gradientUnits="userSpaceOnUse" gradientTransform="translate(468.373 287.536) rotate(90) scale(430.464 id="table-of-contents"><button class="text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 font-medium flex items-center space-x-2 hover:text-gray-900 dark:hover:text-gray-100 transition-colors cursor-pointer"><svg href="#what-is-the-current-state-of-ai" class="break-words py-1 block font-medium hover:text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-300">What is the current state of AI?</a></li><li class="toc-item relative" data-depth="0"><a href="#why-does-ai-need-to-be-on-chain" class="break-words py-1 block font-medium hover:text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-300">Why does dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-300">Top models will be open-source</a></li><li class="toc-item relative" data-depth="0"><a href="#ritual-is-the-conduit-for-crypto-%C3%97-ai" class="break-words py-1 block font-medium hover:text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-300">Ritual is the conduit for Crypto × AI</a></li></ul></div></div></div></div><div class="relative grow box-border flex-col w-full mx-auto px-1 lg:pl-[23.7rem] lg:-ml-12 xl:w-[calc(100%-28rem)]" id="content-area"><header id="header" class="relative leading-none"><div class="mt-0.5 space-y-2.5"><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-start sm:items-center relative gap-2 min-w-0"><h1 id="page-title" class="text-2xl sm:text-3xl text-gray-900 tracking-tight dark:text-gray-200 [overflow-wrap:anywhere] font-bold">Crypto × AI</h1></div></div><div class="mt-2 text-lg prose prose-gray dark:prose-invert [&amp;&gt;*]:[overflow-wrap:anywhere]"><p>The intersection of the most important technologies of our time.</p></div></header><div class="mdx-content relative mt-8 mb-14 prose prose-gray dark:prose-invert [contain:inline-size] isolate" data-page-title="Crypto × AI" data-page-href="/overview/crypto-x-ai" id="content"><hr/>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="what-is-the-current-state-of-ai"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#what-is-the-current-state-of-ai" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">What is the current state of AI?</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">It took ChatGPT just under two months to reach <strong>100 million monthly active
users</strong>. One in every five Americans uses LLMs in their day-to-day life, with
half being under the age of thirty.</span>
<span data-as="p">We are in the early innings of consumer market fit with a Cambrian explosion of
AI applications being built. Yet, the way AI predominantly exists today <strong>is not
sustainable</strong>:</span>
<ol>
<li><strong>Data &amp; compute oligopoly</strong>: The race for better model performance has come
down a <em>moatless</em> tug of war over access to user data and GPU resources.
<a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/opinion/articles/2023-06-02/openai-s-sam-altman-regenerates-the-gilded-age-playbook" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Regulatory capture</a>
and monopolization is becoming the de facto standard.</li>
<li><strong>Closed model monopolies</strong>: The best performing models (see
<a href="https://lmarena.ai/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">model leaderboards</a>) are dominated by centralized
research powerhouses (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc.) unwilling to share their
methodology or open-source their weights.</li>
<li><strong>Alignment autocracy</strong>: Models are subjectively censored by centralized
corporations under the guise of AI safety and fairness.</li>
<li><strong>Privacy violations</strong>: User data, including private conversations, is
commonly
<a href="https://help.openai.com/en/articles/5722486-how-your-data-is-used-to-improve-model-performance" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">used as content for model training</a>,
eroding any notion of privacy.</li>
<li><strong>Arbitrary censorship</strong>: Centralized AI-servicing corporations selectively
censor requests, users, and
<a href="https://www.reuters.com/technology/italy-fines-openai-15-million-euros-over-privacy-rules-breach-2024-12-20/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">even entire nations</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Forced trust</strong>: Users consuming closed-source AI models must trust
operators to run models correctly without manipulating their inputs or
cheating them with worse models.</li>
<li><strong>Limited user preference</strong>: Users have limited choice over optimizing for
speed or cost, instead defaulting to just the hosted services offered by
model providers. Limited competition inhibits cost improvement.</li>
<li><strong>Platform risk</strong>: Developers building on centralized AI
<a href="https://www.businessinsider.com/chatgpt-wrapper-startup-founders-see-risks-of-openai-2023-11" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">face competition</a>
from the providers themselves, risking having their business stolen and
losing their underlying API access.</li>
</ol>
<hr/>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="why-does-ai-need-to-be-on-chain"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#why-does-ai-need-to-be-on-chain" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Why does AI need to be on-chain?</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">It is more crucial than ever to maintain AI systems that are <strong>transparent,
unbiased, and free from undue control</strong>. AI has the power to do significant good
in the hands of many, but without <strong>open access, governance, and ownership</strong>,
may unintentionally do more harm.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="crypto-is-the-only-proven-decentralizing-force"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#crypto-is-the-only-proven-decentralizing-force" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Crypto is the only proven decentralizing force</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">There is no technology in the world with as powerful a claim to decentralization
as crypto.</span>
<span data-as="p">Fundamentally, blockchain networks enable <strong>self-sovereign control of data and
capital</strong>, without reliance on singular intermediaries. The very nature of these
immutable ledgers supports <strong>perpetual verifiability and provenance</strong>.
Naturally, blockchains empower <strong>composability</strong>, letting AI applications
combine, interoperate, and grow intelligence.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="top-models-will-be-open-source"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#top-models-will-be-open-source" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Top models will be open-source</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Open-source LLM model evals have rapidly converged to the performance of
state-of-the-art, closed-source models, closing the gap that existed just two
years ago. Developers now have credible alternatives to break free from reliance
on centralized AI providers.</span>
<span data-as="p">The last decade of social innovation in blockchains has led to tried and tested
mechanisms to <strong>share ownership, distribute control, and govern open-source
software</strong> such as AI models.</span>
<div><div data-name="frame" class="frame p-2 not-prose relative bg-gray-50/50 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden dark:bg-gray-800/25"><div style="background-position:10px 10px" class="absolute inset-0 bg-grid-neutral-200/20 [mask-image:linear-gradient(0deg,#fff,rgba(255,255,255,0.6))] dark:bg-grid-white/5 dark:[mask-image:linear-gradient(0deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.1),rgba(255,255,255,0.5))]"></div><div class="relative rounded-xl overflow-hidden flex justify-center"><span aria-owns="rmiz-modal-" data-rmiz=""><span data-rmiz-content="not-found" style="visibility:visible"><picture class="contents"><img data-path="assets/images/crypto-x-ai.svg" src="https://mintcdn.com/ritualfoundation/a7GImEbJRnhEjeNO/assets/images/crypto-x-ai.svg?fit=max&amp;auto=format&amp;n=a7GImEbJRnhEjeNO&amp;q=85&amp;s=896fe2fa13445c2151ce239a95017019" alt="Crypto × <hr/>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="ritual-is-the-conduit-for-crypto-×-ai"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#ritual-is-the-conduit-for-crypto-×-ai" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Ritual is the conduit for Crypto × AI</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Ritual is purpose-built to decentralize access to AI compute:</span>
<ol>
<li><strong>Enshrined compute</strong>: Ritual
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/ai-primitives/enshrined-ai-models">enshrines AI models</a>, enabling
<strong>ownership</strong> and <strong>provenance</strong>.</li>
<li><strong>Censorship resistant</strong>: Anyone can decentrally
<a class="link" href="/docs/using-ritual/ritual-for-node-runners">join, validate, and contribute</a> to
Ritual.</li>
<li><strong>Composable</strong>: Ritual enables AI composability powering use cases like
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/agents">Smart Agents</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Verifiable AI Provenance</strong>: Ritual enables open- and closed-source model
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/ai-primitives/verifiable-provenance">verifiability</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Privacy</strong>: Cascade powers Ritual’s industry-defining inference privacy.</li>
<li><strong>Modular computational integrity</strong>: Ritual empowers applications to choose
the computational integrity primitive that
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/ai-primitives/modular-computational-integrity">best fits their use case</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Optimized user cost</strong>: Users dictate their speed/cost preference via
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/resonance">Resonance</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Node specialization</strong>: Hardware-optimized nodes specialize in compute via
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/symphony">Symphony</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Developer tools</strong>: <a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/evm++/overview">EVM++</a>,
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/evm++/eip-extensions/overview">EIP Extensions</a>,
<a class="link" href="/docs/architecture/scheduled-transactions">Scheduled Transactions</a>,
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/enshrined-oracles/scheduled-transactions">Enshrined Oracles</a>,
<a class="link" href="/docs/architecture/infernet-to-chain">Infernet</a>,
<a class="link" href="/docs/whats-new/modular-storage">Modular Storage</a>, and
<a class="link" href="/docs/using-ritual/ritual-for-users">more</a> powerful AI application building blocks.</li>
<li><strong>Model monetization</strong>: Ritual enables users to
<a class="link" href="/docs/beyond-crypto-x-ai/model-marketplace">train, track, and trade</a> AI models.</li>
<li><strong>Familiar interface</strong>: Ritual is seamless for both
<a class="link" href="/docs/architecture/infernet-to-chain#chain-as-an-interface">Web2 APIs</a> and Web3
smart contracts.</li>
</ol></div><div class="left-0 right-0 sticky bottom-0 w-full overflow-hidden z-20 pointer-events-none print:hidden"><div class="chat-assistant-floating-input w-full group/assistant-bar relative
